########################################################
### EU scripted effects for new EU 1.2 voting system ###
########################################################

##################################
### EU AI voting modifier vars ###
##################################

EU_update_AI_general_voting_modifiers = {
	hidden_effect = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [FROM.GetTag]: 99_EU_voting_scripted_effects EU_update_AI_general_voting_modifiers"
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = EU_member
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = EU_AI_general_voting_modifier_YES
				value = 50
			}
			### modifiers for voting cheats
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_global_flag = EU_voting_cheat_yes
				}
				add_to_variable = {
					var = EU_AI_general_voting_modifier_YES
					value = 1000 ### ai chance
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_global_flag = EU_voting_cheat_no
				}
				add_to_variable = {
					var = EU_AI_general_voting_modifier_YES
					value = -1000 ### ai chance
				}
			}

			### modifiers for influence of ROOT on all other EU members
			if = {
				limit = {
					ROOT_influence_on_THIS_5_percent = yes
				}
				add_to_variable = {
					var = EU_AI_general_voting_modifier_YES
					value = 5 ### ai chance yes +5 no -5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					ROOT_influence_on_THIS_10_percent = yes
				}
				add_to_variable = {
					var = EU_AI_general_voting_modifier_YES
					value = 5 ### ai chance yes +5 no -5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					ROOT_influence_on_THIS_20_percent = yes
				}
				add_to_variable = {
					var = EU_AI_general_voting_modifier_YES
					value = 10 ### ai chance yes +10 no -10
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					ROOT_influence_on_THIS_30_percent = yes
				}
				add_to_variable = {
					var = EU_AI_general_voting_modifier_YES
					value = 10 ### ai chance yes +10 no -10
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					ROOT_influence_on_THIS_50_percent = yes
				}
				add_to_variable = {
					var = EU_AI_general_voting_modifier_YES
					value = 15 ### ai chance yes +15 no -15
				}
			}
			### modifiers for eurosceptic
			if = {
				limit = {
					THIS = {
						check_variable = {
							var = THIS.eurosceptic
							value = 0.1
							compare = greater_than_or_equals
						}
					}
				}
				add_to_variable = {
					var = EU_AI_general_voting_modifier_YES
					value = -5 ### ai chance yes -5 no +5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					THIS = {
						check_variable = {
							var = THIS.eurosceptic
							value = 0.2
							compare = greater_than_or_equals
						}
					}
				}
				add_to_variable = {
					var = EU_AI_general_voting_modifier_YES
					value = -5 ### ai chance yes -5 no +5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					THIS = {
						check_variable = {
							var = THIS.eurosceptic
							value = 0.3
							compare = greater_than_or_equals
						}
					}
				}
				add_to_variable = {
					var = EU_AI_general_voting_modifier_YES
					value = -5 ### ai chance yes -5 no +5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					THIS = {
						check_variable = {
							var = THIS.eurosceptic
							value = 0.5
							compare = greater_than_or_equals
						}
					}
				}
				add_to_variable = {
					var = EU_AI_general_voting_modifier_YES
					value = -10 ### ai chance yes -10 no +10
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					THIS = {
						check_variable = {
							var = THIS.eurosceptic
							value = 0.7
							compare = greater_than_or_equals
						}
					}
				}
				add_to_variable = {
					var = EU_AI_general_voting_modifier_YES
					value = -20 ### ai chance yes -20 no +20
				}
			}

			### modifiers for gov_resist
			### see focus specific modifiers
			###

			set_variable = {
				var = EU_AI_general_voting_modifier_NO
				value = EU_AI_general_voting_modifier_YES
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				var = EU_AI_general_voting_modifier_NO
				value = -1
			}
		}
	}
}

### modifier for gov_resist

EU_update_AI_focus_EU001_voting_modifier = {
	hidden_effect = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [FROM.GetTag]: 99_EU_voting_scripted_effects EU_update_AI_focus_EU001_voting_modifier"
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = EU_member
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = EU_AI_focus_EU001_voting_modifier_YES
				value = 0
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					THIS = {
						OR = {
							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 1 } ### conservatism
							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 6 } ### Conservative
							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 14 } ### Neutral_conservatism
						}
					}
				}
				add_to_variable = {
					var = EU_AI_focus_EU001_voting_modifier_YES
					value = 0 ### ai chance yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					THIS = {
						OR = {
							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 2 } ### liberalism
							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 16 } ### Neutral_Libertarian
						}
					}
				}
				add_to_variable = {
					var = EU_AI_focus_EU001_voting_modifier_YES
					value = 0 ### ai chance yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					THIS = {
						OR = {
							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 3 } ### socialism
							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 18 } ### neutral_Social
						}
					}
				}
				add_to_variable = {
					var = EU_AI_focus_EU001_voting_modifier_YES
					value = 0 ### ai chance yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					THIS = {
						#OR = {
							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 17 } ### Neutral_green
						#}
					}
				}
				add_to_variable = {
					var = EU_AI_focus_EU001_voting_modifier_YES
					value = 0 ### ai chance yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					THIS = {
						OR = {
							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 4 } ### Communist-State
							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 5 } ### anarchist_communism
							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 19 } ### Neutral_Communism
						}
					}
				}
				add_to_variable = {
					var = EU_AI_focus_EU001_voting_modifier_YES
					value = 0 ### ai chance yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					THIS = {
						OR = {
							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 20 } ### Nat_Populism
							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 21 } ### Nat_Fascism
							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 22 } ### Nat_Autocracy
							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 23 } ### Monarchist
						}
					}
				}
				add_to_variable = {
					var = EU_AI_focus_EU001_voting_modifier_YES
					value = 0 ### ai chance yes
				}
			}
		}
			EU_update_AI_general_voting_modifiers = yes
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = EU_member
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				var = EU_AI_focus_EU001_voting_modifier_YES
				value = EU_AI_general_voting_modifier_YES ### ai chance yes AI_general_voting_modifiers
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = EU_AI_focus_EU001_voting_modifier_NO
				value = EU_AI_focus_EU001_voting_modifier_YES
			}
			multiply_variable = {
				var = EU_AI_focus_EU001_voting_modifier_NO
				value = -1
			}
		}
	}
}

EU_update_AI_focus_EU102_voting_modifier = {
	hidden_effect = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [FROM.GetTag]: 99_EU_voting_scripted_effects EU_update_AI_focus_EU102_voting_modifier"
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = EU_member
			}
			set_variable = {
				var = EU_AI_focus_EU102_voting_modifier_YES
				value = 0
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					THIS = {
						OR = {
							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 1 } ### conservatism
							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 6 } ### Conservative
							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 14 } ### Neutral_conservatism
						}
					}
				}
				add_to_variable = {
					var = EU_AI_focus_EU102_voting_modifier_YES
					value = 10 ### gov_support ### ai chance yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					THIS = {
						OR = {
							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 2 } ### liberalism
							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 16 } ### Neutral_Libertarian
						}
					}
				}
				add_to_variable = {
					var = EU_AI_focus_EU102_voting_modifier_YES
					value = 10 ### gov_support ### ai chance yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					THIS = {
						OR = {
							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 3 } ### socialism
							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 18 } ### neutral_Social
						}
					}
				}
				add_to_variable = {
					var = EU_AI_focus_EU102_voting_modifier_YES
					value = 25 ### gov_strong_support ### ai chance yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					THIS = {
						#OR = {
							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 17 } ### Neutral_green
						#}
					}
				}
				add_to_variable = {
					var = EU_AI_focus_EU102_voting_modifier_YES
					value = 25 ### gov_strong_support ### ai chance yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					THIS = {
						OR = {
							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 4 } ### Communist-State
							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 5 } ### anarchist_communism
							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 19 } ### Neutral_Communism
						}
					}
				}
				add_to_variable = {
					var = EU_AI_focus_EU102_voting_modifier_YES
					value = 25 ### gov_strong_support ### ai chance yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					THIS = {
						OR = {
							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 20 } ### Nat_Populism
							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 21 } ### Nat_Fascism
							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 22 } ### Nat_Autocracy
							is_in_array = { ruling_party = 23 } ### Monarchist
						}
					}
				}
				add_to_variable = {
					var = EU_AI_focus_EU102_voting_modifier_YES
					value = -25 ### gov_strong_resist ### ai chance yes
				}
			}
		}
			EU_update_AI_general_voting_modifiers = yes
		every_country = {

					}

		focus_EU610_voting_prediction_EUpopRatio_Undecided = yes
		focus_EU610_voting_prediction_EUpopRatio_NO = yes
	}

	if = {
		limit = {
			focus_EU611_draft = yes
			NOT = {
				focus_EU611_accepted = yes
			}
		}
		focus_EU611_voting_prediction_total_YES_votes = yes
		focus_EU611_voting_prediction_total_Undecided_votes = yes
		focus_EU611_voting_prediction_total_NO_votes = yes
		focus_EU611_voting_prediction_EUpopRatio_YES = yes
		focus_EU611_voting_prediction_EUpopRatio_Undecided = yes
		focus_EU611_voting_prediction_EUpopRatio_NO = yes
	}
}

		value = 0
	}
	every_country = {
		limit = {
			has_idea = EU_member
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_idea = EUU_voting_rights_suspended
				}
				check_variable = {
					var = EU_AI_focus_EU001_voting_modifier_YES
					value = 65
					compare = greater_than_or_equals
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				var = global.focus_EU001_voting_prediction_total_YES_votes
				value = 1
			}
		}
	}
}

### EU001 ###

focus_EU001_result = {
	if = { # Unanimity - yes
		limit = {
			has_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting
			check_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUvoteYes
				value = global.var_EUvoteTotal
				compare = equals
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = focus_EU001_yes
		set_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting_YES
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = EU_voted
				NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU001 }
			}
			news_event = {
				id = EUvote_news.2
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU001 }
			news_event = {
				id = EUvote.3001
			}
		}
	}
	else = { # Unanimity - no
		set_country_flag = focus_EU001_no
		set_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting_NO
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = EU_voted
				NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU001 }
			}
			news_event = {
				id = EUvote_news.2
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU001 }
			news_event = {
				id = EUvote.4001
			}
		}
	}
}

focus_EU001_QMV_result = {
	if = { # QMV - yes
		limit = {
			has_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting
			check_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUvoteYes
				value = 0.55
				compare = greater_than_or_equals
			}
			check_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUpopYes
				value = 0.65
				compare = greater_than_or_equals
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = focus_EU001_QMV_yes
		set_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_YES
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = EU_voted
				NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU001_QMV }
			}
			news_event = {
				id = EUvote_news.2
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU001_QMV }
			news_event = {
				id = EUvote.3001
			}
		}
	}
	else = { # QMV - no
		set_country_flag = focus_EU001_QMV_no
		set_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_NO
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = EU_voted
				NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU001_QMV }
			}
			news_event = {
				id = EUvote_news.2
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU001_QMV }
			news_event = {
				id = EUvote.4001
			}
		}
	}
}

### EU100 ###

focus_EU100_result = {
	if = { # Unanimity - yes
		limit = {
			has_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting
			check_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUvoteYes
				value = global.var_EUvoteTotal
				compare = equals
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = focus_EU100_yes
		set_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting_YES
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = EU_voted
				NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU100 }
			}
			news_event = {
				id = EUvote_news.2
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU100 }
			news_event = {
				id = EUvote.3100
			}
		}
	}
	else = { # Unanimity - no
		set_country_flag = focus_EU100_no
		set_global_flag = EU_unanimity_voting_NO
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = EU_voted
				NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU100 }
			}
			news_event = {
				id = EUvote_news.2
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU100 }
			news_event = {
				id = EUvote.4100
			}
		}
	}
}

focus_EU100_QMV_result = {
	if = { # QMV - yes
		limit = {
			has_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting
			check_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUvoteYes
				value = 0.55
				compare = greater_than_or_equals
			}
			check_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUpopYes
				value = 0.65
				compare = greater_than_or_equals
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = focus_EU100_QMV_yes
		set_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_YES
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = EU_voted
				NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU100_QMV }
			}
			news_event = {
				id = EUvote_news.2
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU100_QMV }
			news_event = {
				id = EUvote.3100
			}
		}
	}
	else = { # QMV - no
		set_country_flag = focus_EU100_QMV_no
		set_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_NO
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = EU_voted
				NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU100_QMV }
			}
			news_event = {
				id = EUvote_news.2
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU100_QMV }
			news_event = {
				id = EUvote.4100
			}
		}
	}
}

		set_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_YES
		every_country = {

		}

			news_event = {

focus_EU605_QMV_result = {
	if = { # QMV - yes
		limit = {
			has_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting
			check_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUvoteYes
				value = 0.55
				compare = greater_than_or_equals
			}
			check_variable = {
				var = global.var_EUpopYes
				value = 0.65
				compare = greater_than_or_equals
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = focus_EU605_QMV_yes
		set_global_flag = EU_qualified_majority_voting_YES
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = EU_voted
				NOT = { has_country_flag = focus_EU605_QMV }
			}
			news_event = {
				id = EUvote_news.2
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = focus_EU605_QMV }

		}
	}
